09 Aug 2017 19:03:33 : Achievement Heaven, kat, GamerKatland#1817, yui autorole help
09 Aug 2017 19:03:33 : Achievement Heaven, kat, Yui (ユイ)#2222, Use `Yui autorole` to check if autorole is enabled and which roles are automatically assigned.
If it's disabled and you wish to enable it, use `Yui autorole enable`.
To assign a new automatic role, you can use `Yui autorole add <role>`.
For example: `Yui autorole add Peasant`.

For reporting you can use `Yui autorole report` or `Yui autorole shhh` to disable it.
Reporting will tell you if the bot doesn't have the correct permissions when a member joins.

IMPORTANT: Make sure Yui's default role 'Yui (ユイ)' is above the roles you want to automatically assign!
